Source Code

These source code files are an attempted reconstruction of Sundance revision 306, the Apollo 9 LM (Lunar Module) AGC (Apollo Guidance Computer) flight software, created from binary dumps of original core rope program modules, as follows:
  • B1 — Revision 292
  • B2 — Revision 302
  • B3 — Revision 302
  • B4 — Revision 302
  • B5 — Revision 292
  • B6 — Revision 306
These dumps were then modified using memos, checklists, observed address changes, and the Sundance GSOPs to get the entire program to match Sundance revision 306 as closely as possible. Without more information, it is not possible to say how close it actually is; however, this code should be quite close. It is capable of flying the whole Apollo 9 mission using the original checklists and padload. Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Sundance are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

019689,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
019690,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
019691,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of an attempt to reconstruct Sundance revision 306
019692,000005:                                                                                                  ##              as closely as possible with available information. Sundance
019693,000006:                                                                                                  ##              306 is the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
019694,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 9. This program was created
019695,000008:                                                                                                  ##              using the mixed-revision SundanceXXX as a starting point, and
019696,000009:                                                                                                  ##              pulling back features from Luminary 69 believed to have been
019697,000010:                                                                                                  ##              added based on memos, checklists, observed address changes,
019698,000011:                                                                                                  ##              or the Sundance GSOPs.
019699,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
019700,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
019701,000014:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
019702,000015:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-07-24 MAS  Created from SundanceXXX.
019703,000016:                                                                                                  ##              2020-07-29 MAS  Changed R22 restart protection to be closer
019704,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              to Luminary 69.
019705,000018: 
019706,000019: 
019707,000020:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
019708,000021:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
019709,000022:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
019710,000023:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
019711,000024:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
019712,000025: 
019713,000026:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
019714,000027:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
019715,000028:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
019716,000029:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
019717,000030:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
019718,000031: 
019719,000032:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
019720,000033:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
019721,000034:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
019722,000035:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
019723,000036:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
019724,000037:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
019725,000038:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
019726,000039:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
019727,000040:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
019728,000041:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
019729,000042:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
019730,000043:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
019731,000044:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
019732,000045:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
019733,000046:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
019734,000047:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
019735,000048:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
019736,000049:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
019737,000050:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
019738,000051:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
019739,000052:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
019740,000053:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
019741,000054:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
019742,000055:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
019743,000056: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
019744,000057: 
019745,000058: 33,2000                                           BANK     33                                    
019746,000059: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
019747,000060: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
019748,000061: 
019749,000062: 24,2000  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
019750,000063: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

020032,000345:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020033,000346:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
020034,000347:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
020035,000348:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
020036,000349:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020037,000350: 
020038,000351:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
020039,000352:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
020040,000353:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
020041,000354:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
020042,000355:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020043,000356:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
020044,000357:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
020045,000358:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
020046,000359:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
020047,000360:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
020048,000361:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
020049,000362:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
020050,000363:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
020051,000364:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
020052,000365:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
020053,000366:                                                                                                  #    NONE

020320,000633:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
020321,000634:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020322,000635:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020323,000636:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
020324,000637:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020325,000638: 
020326,000639:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
020327,000640:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
020328,000641:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020329,000642:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
020330,000643:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
020331,000644:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
020332,000645:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
020333,000646:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
020334,000647:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
020335,000648:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
020336,000649:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
020337,000650:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
020338,000651:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
020339,000652:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
020340,000653:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -

020342,000655:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION

020423,000736:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
020424,000737:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020425,000738:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2

020427,000740:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020428,000741: 
020429,000742:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
020430,000743:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -

020436,000749:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
020437,000750:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23

020491,000804:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
020492,000805:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020493,000806:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020494,000807:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
020495,000808:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020496,000809: 
020497,000810:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
020498,000811:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
020499,000812:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
020500,000813:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
020501,000814:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
020502,000815:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
020503,000816:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
020504,000817:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
020505,000818:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020506,000819:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
020507,000820:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
020508,000821:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
020509,000822:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
020510,000823:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
020511,000824:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
020512,000825:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
020513,000826:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
020514,000827:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
020515,000828:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
020516,000829:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
020517,000830:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020518,000831:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
020519,000832:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020520,000833:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
020521,000834: 24,3035  E7,1720                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
020522,000835: 24,3035                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
020523,000836: 24,3035           05566        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
020524,000837: 24,3036           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
020525,000838: 24,3037           35030        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
020526,000839: 24,3040           55720                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
020527,000840: 24,3041           55721                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
020528,000841: 24,3042           55722                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
020529,000842: 24,3043           05423        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG

020531,000844: 24,3045           33117                           CAF      V16N80

020533,000846: 24,3047           20414                           CADR     PRIODSPR

020582,000895:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
020583,000896:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020584,000897:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO : 3                      DATE : 4-11-67
020585,000898:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY : P VOLANTE  SDC
020586,000899: 
020587,000900: 
020588,000901:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
020589,000902:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
020590,000903:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED

020685,000998:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020686,000999:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
020687,001000:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
020688,001001:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
020689,001002:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
020690,001003:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
020691,001004:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
020692,001005:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
020693,001006:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
020694,001007:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
020695,001008:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
020696,001009:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
020697,001010:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
020698,001011:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
020699,001012:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.

020761,001074:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
020762,001075: 
020763,001076:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020764,001077:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
020765,001078:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
020766,001079:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
020767,001080:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
020768,001081:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
020769,001082:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
020770,001083:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
020771,001084:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
020772,001085:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
020773,001086:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
020774,001087:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
020775,001088:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
020776,001089:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
020777,001090:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
020778,001091:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
020779,001092:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
020780,001093:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
020781,001094:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
020782,001095:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL

020850,001163: 
020851,001164: 
020852,001165:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
020853,001166: 
020854,001167:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020855,001168: 
020856,001169:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
020857,001170:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
020858,001171:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
020859,001172:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
020860,001173:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
020861,001174:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
020862,001175:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
020863,001176:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
020864,001177:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
020865,001178:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
020866,001179:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
020867,001180:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
020868,001181: 
020869,001182:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
020870,001183:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
020871,001184:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
020872,001185: 
020873,001186:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020874,001187:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
020875,001188: 
020876,001189:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
020877,001190: 
020878,001191:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
020879,001192:                                                                                                  #  NONE
020880,001193: 
020881,001194:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
020882,001195: 
020883,001196:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
020884,001197: 
020885,001198: 24,3120                                           BANK     24                                    
020886,001199: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
020887,001200: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
020888,001201: 
020889,001202: 25,2053  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020890,001203: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
020891,001204: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
020892,001205: 25,2054           05271                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
020893,001206: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
020894,001207: 25,2056           45026                           CS       BIT1                                  
020895,001208: 25,2057           71101                           MASK     RADMODES                              
020896,001209: 25,2060           55101                           TS       RADMODES                              
020897,001210: 25,2061           15331                           TCF      TASKOVER                              
020898,001211: 
020899,001212:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
020900,001213: 
020901,001214:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020902,001215:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
020903,001216:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
020904,001217:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
020905,001218:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
020906,001219:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
020907,001220:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
020908,001221:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
020909,001222:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
020910,001223:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
020911,001224:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
020912,001225:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
020913,001226:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
020914,001227:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
020915,001228:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
020916,001229:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
020917,001230: 
020918,001231:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
020919,001232:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020920,001233:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
020921,001234:

020970,001283: 
020971,001284:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
020972,001285:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020973,001286:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
020974,001287:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
020975,001288:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
020976,001289:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
020977,001290:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
020978,001291:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
020979,001292:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
020980,001293:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
020981,001294:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
020982,001295:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
020983,001296:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
020984,001297:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
020985,001298:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
020986,001299:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
020987,001300:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
020988,001301:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
020989,001302:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
020990,001303:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
020991,001304:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
020992,001305:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
020993,001306:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
020994,001307:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
020995,001308: 
020996,001309:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
020997,001310:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
020998,001311:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
020999,001312: 
021000,001313:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021001,001314:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
021002,001315:

021058,001371:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
021059,001372: 
021060,001373:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
021061,001374:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
021062,001375:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
021063,001376:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
021064,001377:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
021065,001378:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
021066,001379:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
021067,001380:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
021068,001381:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
021069,001382:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
021070,001383:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
021071,001384:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
021072,001385:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
021073,001386:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
021074,001387:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
021075,001388:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
021076,001389:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
021077,001390:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
021078,001391:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
021079,001392:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
021080,001393: 
021081,001394:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021082,001395:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
021083,001396:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
021084,001397:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
021085,001398:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.

021138,001451:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
021139,001452: 
021140,001453:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021141,001454:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
021142,001455:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
021143,001456:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
021144,001457:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
021145,001458:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
021146,001459:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
021147,001460:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
021148,001461:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
021149,001462:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
021150,001463:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
021151,001464:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
021152,001465:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
021153,001466:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
021154,001467:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
021155,001468: 
021156,001469:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
021157,001470:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
021158,001471:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
021159,001472:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
021160,001473:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
021161,001474: 
021162,001475:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021163,001476:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES

021225,001538:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
021226,001539: 
021227,001540:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021228,001541:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
021229,001542:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
021230,001543:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
021231,001544:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
021232,001545:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
021233,001546:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
021234,001547:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
021235,001548:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
021236,001549:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
021237,001550:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
021238,001551:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
021239,001552:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
021240,001553:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
021241,001554: 
021242,001555:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021243,001556:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
021244,001557:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
021245,001558: 
021246,001559:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021247,001560:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
021248,001561:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
021249,001562: 
021250,001563:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021251,001564:                                                                                                  #  MAGSUB
021252,001565: 
021253,001566:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
021254,001567:                                                                                                  #  NONE
021255,001568: 
021256,001569:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
021257,001570: 
021258,001571:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+1 (ALWAYS)                                                     SIRED VALUES. RUPT MUST BE INHIBITED.

021273,001586: 25,2300           57322                           XCH      LASTYCMD                              #  LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD

021324,001637: 25,2350           13502                           TCF      ENDRADAR                              
021325,001638: 
021326,001639: 25,2351           02001        BIT11+1            OCT      02001                                 
021327,001640: 
021328,001641:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
021329,001642: 
021330,001643:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021331,001644:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
021332,001645:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
021333,001646:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
021334,001647:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
021335,001648:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
021336,001649:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
021337,001650:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
021338,001651:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
021339,001652:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
021340,001653:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
021341,001654:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
021342,001655:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
021343,001656:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
021344,001657:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
021345,001658:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
021346,001659:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
021347,001660:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
021348,001661:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
021349,001662:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
021350,001663:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
021351,001664:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
021352,001665:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
021353,001666: 
021354,001667:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021355,001668:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
021356,001669:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
021357,001670:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
021358,001671:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
021359,001672: 
021360,001673:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021361,001674:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
021362,001675: 
021363,001676:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021364,001677:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
021365,001678:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
021366,001679: 
021367,001680:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
021368,001681:                                                                                                  #     NONE
021369,001682: 
021370,001683:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
021371,001684: 
021372,001685:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
021373,001686:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
021374,001687:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
021375,001688: 
021376,001689: 25,2352           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
021377,001690: 25,2353           01116                                    DESRET                                
021378,001691: 25,2354           00271                                    RRNBSW                                
021379,001692: 25,2355           77624                           CALL                                           #  COMPUTES SINES AND COSINES, ORDER Y Z X
021380,001693: 25,2356           47335                                    CDUTRIG                               
021381,001694: 25,2357           45175                           VLOAD    CALL                                  #  LOAD VECTOR AND CALL TRANSFORMATION
021382,001695: 25,2360           01105                                    RRTARGET                              
021383,001696: 25,2361           47477                                    *SMNB*

021386,001699: 25,2363           26105                                    RRANGLES                              #  ALTERNATE MODE.
021387,001700: 25,2364           77776                           EXIT                                           
021388,001701:

021390,001703: 25,2366           04540                           TC       RRLIMCHK

021392,001705: 25,2370           02373                           TC       +3                                    #  NOT IN CURRENT MODE

021400,001713:

021403,001716: 25,2401           75017                           MASK     SURFFBIT                              #  CHECK IF ON LUNAR SURFACE

021406,001719: 25,2404           02444                           TC       NODESSM                               #  NOT ON MOON-CALL FOR ATTITUDE MANEUVER
021407,001720: 
021408,001721:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
021409,001722: 
021410,001723:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
021411,001724:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
021412,001725:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
021413,001726:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
021414,001727:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
021415,001728:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
021416,001729:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
021417,001730:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
021418,001731:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
021419,001732:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
021420,001733:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
021421,001734:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
021422,001735:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
021423,001736:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
021424,001737:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
021425,001738:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
021426,001739:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
021427,001740:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
021428,001741:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
021429,001742:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
021430,001743:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
021431,001744: 
021432,001745:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021433,001746:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.

021574,001887: 25,2546           03512        20.5DEGS           DEC      .11389                                
021575,001888: 
021576,001889:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
021577,001890: 
021578,001891:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021579,001892:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
021580,001893:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
021581,001894:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
021582,001895:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
021583,001896:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
021584,001897:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
021585,001898:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
021586,001899:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
021587,001900:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
021588,001901:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
021589,001902:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
021590,001903:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
021591,001904:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
021592,001905:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
021593,001906:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
021594,001907:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
021595,001908:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
021596,001909:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
021597,001910:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
021598,001911:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
021599,001912:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
021600,001913:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
021601,001914:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
021602,001915:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
021603,001916:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
021604,001917: 
021605,001918:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021606,001919:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
021607,001920:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
021608,001921:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
021609,001922: 
021610,001923:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021611,001924:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
021612,001925: 
021613,001926:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021614,001927:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
021615,001928: 
021616,001929:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
021617,001930: 
021618,001931:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
021619,001932:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
021620,001933: 
021621,001934:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
021622,001935:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
021623,001936:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
021624,001937: 
021625,001938: 25,2547           41101        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

021632,001945: 25,2555           00062                           DEC      50         B-14

021636,001949: 25,2560           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  OUT OF BOUNDS. IF SO, THIS BIT SHOWS A
021637,001950: 25,2561           12613                           TCF      BADDES                                #  REPOSITION TO BE IN PROGRESS.

021645,001958: 25,2567           75015                           MASK     BIT10                                 #  PROBLEM (DATA GOOD IF LOCK-ON WANTED OR
021646,001959: 25,2570           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  WITHIN LIMITS IF NOT). IF SO, EXIT AFTER
021647,001960: 25,2571           13502                           TCF      ENDRADAR                              #  CHECKING RR CDU FAIL.
