021683,001996: 
021684,001997:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
021685,001998: 
021686,001999:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021687,002000:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
021688,002001:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
021689,002002:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
021690,002003:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
021691,002004:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
021692,002005:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
021693,002006:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
021694,002007:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
021695,002008:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE
021696,002009:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
021697,002010:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
021698,002011:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE
021699,002012:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
021700,002013:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
021701,002014:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
021702,002015:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
021703,002016:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
021704,002017:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
021705,002018:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
021706,002019:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
021707,002020:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
021708,002021:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
021709,002022:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
021710,002023:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
021711,002024:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
021712,002025:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
021713,002026:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
021714,002027:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
021715,002028:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
021716,002029:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
021717,002030:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
021718,002031:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
021719,002032:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
021720,002033:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
021721,002034:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
021722,002035:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
021723,002036:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
021724,002037: 
021725,002038:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021726,002039:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
021727,002040: 
021728,002041:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021729,002042:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
021730,002043:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
021731,002044: 
021732,002045:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021733,002046:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
021734,002047: 
021735,002048:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
021736,002049:                                                                                                  #  NONE
021737,002050: 
021738,002051:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
021739,002052: 
021740,002053:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)

022448,002761: 
022449,002762:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
022450,002763:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
022451,002764: 
022452,002765: 
022453,002766:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022454,002767: 
022455,002768:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
022456,002769:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
022457,002770:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
022458,002771: 
022459,002772:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
022460,002773: 
022461,002774: 
022462,002775:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
022463,002776: 
022464,002777: 
022465,002778:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
022466,002779: 
022467,002780:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
022468,002781:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
022469,002782:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
022470,002783:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
022471,002784:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
022472,002785: 
022473,002786: 
022474,002787:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
022475,002788: 
022476,002789:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
022477,002790:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
022478,002791: 
022479,002792: 
022480,002793:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
022481,002794:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
022482,002795: 
022483,002796: 
022484,002797:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
022485,002798:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
022486,002799: 
022487,002800:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
022488,002801: 
022489,002802:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
022490,002803:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
022491,002804:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
022492,002805:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
022493,002806:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
022494,002807: 
022495,002808: 
022496,002809:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022497,002810: 
022498,002811:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:
022499,002812: 
022500,002813:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE

022683,002996:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
022684,002997:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
022685,002998:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
022686,002999: 
022687,003000:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022688,003001: 
022689,003002:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
022690,003003:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
022691,003004:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
022692,003005: 
022693,003006:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022694,003007:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
022695,003008:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
022696,003009:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
022697,003010:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
022698,003011:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
022699,003012:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
022700,003013: 
022701,003014: 
022702,003015:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022703,003016:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
022704,003017:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
022705,003018: 
022706,003019:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022707,003020:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
022708,003021:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
022709,003022:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
022710,003023:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
022711,003024:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
022712,003025: 
022713,003026: 
022714,003027:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022715,003028:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
022716,003029:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
022717,003030:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
022718,003031:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
022719,003032:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
022720,003033:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
022721,003034:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
022722,003035:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
022723,003036:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
022724,003037:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
022725,003038:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
022726,003039:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
022727,003040:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
022728,003041:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
022729,003042: 
022730,003043:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022731,003044:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
022732,003045:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

023079,003392: 26,3133           50556                                    R22LEM93                              
023080,003393:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023081,003394: 
023082,003395:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
023083,003396:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
023084,003397:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023085,003398: 
023086,003399:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023087,003400:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
023088,003401:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
023089,003402: 
023090,003403:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023091,003404:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
023092,003405:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
023093,003406:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
023094,003407:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
023095,003408:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
023096,003409: 
023097,003410:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023098,003411:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
023099,003412:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
023100,003413:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
023101,003414:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
023102,003415:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
023103,003416:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
023104,003417: 
023105,003418: 26,3134           77624        LSR22.4            CALL                                           
023106,003419: 26,3135           27362                                    INTSTALL                              
023107,003420: 26,3136           43014                           SET      CLEAR                                 
023108,003421: 26,3137           01472                                    STATEFLG                              
023109,003422: 26,3140           01674                                    VINTFLAG                              #  CALL TO GET LM POS + VEL IN REF COORD.
023110,003423: 26,3141           77624                           CALL                                           
023111,003424: 26,3142           55176                                    INTGRCAL                              
023112,003425: 26,3143           77624                           CALL                                           
023113,003426: 26,3144           11057                                    GRP2PC                                
023114,003427: 26,3145           45014                           CLEAR    CALL                                  
023115,003428: 26,3146           02666                                    DMENFLG                               #  SET MATRIX SIZE TO 6X6 FOR INCORP
023116,003429: 26,3147           27362                                    INTSTALL                              
023117,003430: 26,3150           46145                           DLOAD    BHIZ                                  #  IS THIS FIRST TIME THROUGH
023118,003431: 26,3151           03450                                    MARKCTR                               
023119,003432: 26,3152           55165                                    INITWMX6                              #  YES. INITIALIZE 6X6 W-MATRIX
023120,003433: 26,3153           43014                           CLEAR    SET                                   
023121,003434: 26,3154           01675                                    D6OR9FLG                              
023122,003435: 26,3155           01476                                    DIM0FLAG                              
023123,003436: 26,3156           43014                           SET      CLEAR                                 
023124,003437: 26,3157           01474                                    VINTFLAG                              
023125,003438: 26,3160           01673                                    INTYPFLG                              
023126,003439: 26,3161           77624                           CALL                                           
023127,003440: 26,3162           55176                                    INTGRCAL                              
023128,003441: 26,3163           77650                           GOTO

023229,003542:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
023230,003543: 
023231,003544:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY
023232,003545:                                                                                                  #  RXZ = (SQRT (1-SINTHETA**2))RLC

023234,003547:                                                                                                  #   ULC IN ULC, PD0
023235,003548:                                                                                                  #   RLC IN PD36D

023288,003601: 
023289,003602:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
023290,003603:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
023291,003604: 
023292,003605: 
023293,003606:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023294,003607: 
023295,003608:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
023296,003609:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
023297,003610:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
023298,003611:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
023299,003612: 
023300,003613: 
023301,003614:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
023302,003615: 
023303,003616: 
023304,003617:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023305,003618: 
023306,003619:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
023307,003620:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
023308,003621:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
023309,003622:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
023310,003623:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
023311,003624: 
023312,003625: 
023313,003626:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
023314,003627: 
023315,003628: 
023316,003629:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023317,003630: 
023318,003631:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
023319,003632:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
023320,003633:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
023321,003634: 
023322,003635:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023323,003636:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
023324,003637:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
023325,003638:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023326,003639: 
023327,003640:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
023328,003641:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT

023331,003644:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
023332,003645: 
023333,003646: 26,3362                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24
